Absolutely the best stromboli ever!

<Pics>None< /Pics><name>Joshua Salgado<//name><Gmap_id>0x80dc01ff6068d205:0x77899005f8a18e4< /Gmap_id>< userid>
114947495758966295252<//userid>
<rating>4<//rating>< Review>
Have had my eyes on this place for some time! Was pretty excited to see they had finally opened. First impression was the decor was pretty nice, the wall artwork definitely catches the eye. The menu is pretty expansive, even offering chicken wings (which weren't half bad.) I went with the "Good Ol Burger", which was pretty tasty. The beef is certainly of good quality, and the toasted brioche bun had the right amount of bite to it. The french fries left something to be desired, and the portion could have been larger, but they were hot and fresh with the right amount of salt so no real complaints there. Cost is a little high for the area, but for the quality of ingredients is more than acceptable. I will definitely be returning in the future.
PROS: Good quality for the price, food is fresh and tasty, diverse offerings without feeling hipster
CONS: Could have been more generous with the fries, for a place with "cheese" in the name the cheese plate offerings weren't much
OVERALL: I would definitely recommend this place. Nice to have a proper burger joint in Clairemont.<//Review>

The website clearly says to come to the club so you can meet with the manager in person. I left my name and number at the front desk but no one has called me. She didn't even offer me an application.

So today I applied online for Deja Vu NoHo, I received an email then I called and spoke with Sharon - she was very nice, professional and friendly. I told her what happened at my last attempt and she told me to come up to the club tonight after 5 to speak with Mike because the managers like to see you and your personality. I asked Sharon do any black women work there, she said no.

I think this is the issue with Deja Vu. I don't think they want black women working as waitresses or dancers. I say this because of my 1st experience with the downtown club and to find out there are no brown skinned dancers or waitresses at NoHo gives that vibe.

I'm just trying to make some money and have fun while doing it. I'm attractive, sexy, curvy AND I have an outgoing personality. Not to mention that I'm a huge fan of Larry Flynt's Hustler Casino in Gardena - I play baccarat here and I love their VIP room.

Sharon invited me to come to the club tonight but I will not be going - NoHo is not around the corner from me. I'm in LA and I don't want to waste my time and my gas and I don't want to be disappointed again. I guess I'll keep looking. ~LeLe~</text>

< Review>
The first time I went in this shop, I talked with Jim, who is more informed about frames and lenses and fits and sizing than anyone I'd ever talked to before. He spent at least 30 minutes with me showing me different frames that might work for my face, and explaining why so I could understand and apply that information to other frames. He also suggested I look into VSP vision insurance and do some math to see if it would save me money in purchasing frames, and said he'd be happy to sit down and do all the calculations with me once I figure out what plans I could get.
I needed to absorb that information, and when I came back another day to narrow down frame choices and figure out insurance, I spoke with Maria. Maria, equally as knowledgeable, ended up picking out the frames I eventually purchased, and has spent lots of time over 3-4 visits answering all my questions about the frames and pricing, and even taking pictures so I could look at the frames at home.
The frames are more expensive than most places I've seen, but with insurance, the total came out to something I could afford. They both, Jim and Maria, have also been able to adjust my glasses and sunglasses in a way that made them fit better than anyone I'd ever gone to before (and I've tried a lot of places!). I definitely can't afford multiple pairs here, but when I need a new pair of quality frames, I will definitely return!<//Review>

< Text>
I've had good experiences with this office. They were the ones who removed the mercury from past tooth fillings and discovered a cavity on an X-ray that my previous dentist had missed.  For this visit I had scheduled due to some teeth sensitivity (brushing too hard) and some discomfort chewing. I liked how the problem was isolated to my gums and thank God my teeth seemed to be OK (an X-ray revealed no issues). So the issue was taking care of the current teeth sensitivity while the gums heal. I was given the options of a filling or something called  I-M paste. My insurance wouldn't cover a filling since this area was previously taken care of and it wasn't over 24 months yet. I'm glad that I checked the ingredients of the I-M paste as it contains casein and I have to be dairy-free. When I asked if there were any other alternatives I was offered ozone treatment that would help heal the tubules and mitigate the discomfort.  This seemed the best option since it was quick (less than 5 minutes) and painless. I had originally leaned toward a filling but wasn't guaranteed that it would work since the issue was on the side of my teeth.  I'm wondering why the ozone option wasn't presented at the beginning when talking about treatments? I may have given the impression I was concerned about cost but if it is effective and quick, then it's worth it to me. 2 days later my teeth sensitivity is still being kept at bay so I am happy.</Text>
